 They are hoping for better lives and better employment opportunities, but this is not the case
 rahul ne bijepi par nafrat failaane kaa bhi aarope lagaaya
 The Congress Vice President said that the society is dividing by the ideology of the Sangh and the BJP
 alpsankhyakon or daliton main dar kaa maahaul paidaa ho rahaa he
 Kannada organizations announce the bandh; Rahul Gandhi is coming to Bangalore at a time when protests are being held in Karnataka over the water problem
 kannada sanghathanon ne mahadaayi nadi ke pani ko lekar goa ke saath chal rahe vivaad ke khilaaf somvaar ko karnataka band kaa elaan kiya he
 Organizations demand that the government should resolve this issue quickly and also waive off farmers' loans
 1
 The present system of pay band and grade pay has been abolished and a new pay structure has been approved as per the recommendation of the Commission
 ab se karmchaaree ke darje kaa nirdhaaran pe matrix main uske str ke aadhaar par hoga, jabaki abhi tak grad pe ke anusaar iskaa nirdhaaran hota tha
 Different pay structures are designed for civil (civilian), defense personnel and military nursing service
 in sanrachanaon ke peeche siddhant or tark ek samaan hai
 2
 sabhi vartmaan staron ko naye dhaanche main samahit kar diya gaya he
 No new levels have been introduced nor has any levels been removed
 vetan sanrachana ke har str par nunatam vetan tay karne ke liye suvyavasthikaran ke suchakank ko manjuuri di gai he, jo varishthata kram main har kadam par badhati bhoomika, jimmedaari or javabdehi par nirbhar karata he
 3
 nunatam vetan ko 7000 rupee se badhaakar 18000 rupee prati maah kar diya gaya he
 The starting salary of any newly appointed employee at the minimum level will now be Rs 18000, while the initial salary of a newly appointed 'class I' officer will be Rs 56100
 yah 1:3
 a contraction ratio of 12 indicates that the salary of any directly recruited 'class I' officer will be three times the salary of a newly appointed employee
 4
 2 for the purpose of amendment of salary and pension
 57 kaa fitment factor vetan sanrachanaon main shaamil sabhi staron par lagu hoga
 At least 14 on 1 January 2016 in the salary / pension of all government employees / pensioners after inclusion of DA at the prevailing rate
 29 pratishat kii badhat darj ho jaaegi
 5
 vetan vruddhi kii dar ko 3 pratishat par barkaraar rakhaa gaya he
 Employees will be benefited in future due to higher basic salary, because the annual increase in their salary in future will be 2 as compared to present
 57 guna zyada hogi
 6
 cabinet ne str 13e (brigadier) ke liye suvyavasthikaran suchakank main vruddhi kar or str 12e (le
 Colonel), 13 (colonel) and 13A (brigadier) have further improved the Defense related pay structure by ensuring additional levels, so that parity with Joint Armed Police Forces (CAPF) counterparts at the highest rung of the respective levels
 Can be brought 7
 Certain other decisions have also been taken to affect various employees, including Defense and Joint Armed Police Forces (CAPF) personnel, including the following
 • gracuty kii seemaa 10 lakh rupee se badhaakar 20 lakh rupee kar di gai he
 Whenever DA is increased by 50 percent, the limit of gratuity will increase by 25 percent
 • asainya evam raksha carmikon ke liye anugrah raashi ekamusth muaavje ke bhugtan hetu ek aam vyavastha kii gai he, jo unke parijanon ko dey hoga or iske tahat vartmaan daron ko vibhinn shreniyon ke liye 10-20 lakh rupee se badhaakar 25-45 lakh rupee kar diya gaya he
 • For various categories of personnel of the defense forces, the rates of military service pay have been revised from Rs 1000, 2000, 4200 and 6000 to Rs 3600, 5200, 10800 and 15500 respectively
 8
 The cabinet gave the advance amount related to housing construction
7
 50 lakh rupee se badhaakar 25 lakh rupee karne sambandhi ayog kii sifarish ko bhi manjuuri de di he
 4 interest free advances have been retained to ensure that employees do not face any problems, including advances for medical treatment, TA for tour / transfer, TA for the family of deceased employees and LTC
 anya sabhi byaaj mukt agrimon ko samaapt kar diya gaya he
 9
 cabinet ne centre sarkaar karmchaaree samooh beemaa yojana (sijiijiies) main kiye jane vaale masik anshdaan main baari vruddhi karne kii sifarish ko bhi na maanane kaa nirnay liya he, jaisi ki ayog ne sifarish kii thi
 The comments 10
 The Commission has taken into consideration 196 present allowances in total and has recommended abolition of 51 allowances and incorporating 37 allowances with a view to rationalizing them
 11
 According to the estimate made by the seventh CPC, the implementation of all its recommendations in 2016-17 would entail an additional financial burden of Rs 1,02,100 crore

 6
 The Cabinet has increased the Streamlining Index to Level 13A (brig) and Level 12A (lay
 karnal), 13 (karnal) or 13e (brigadier) main atirikt str (stage) sunishchit karke raksha sambandhi vetan sanrachana ko or behatar kar diya he, taaki sambandhit staron ke adhiktam paaydaan par sanyukt sashastr police bal (siepief) ke samakakshon ke saath samta laai ja sake
 7
 raksha or sanyukt sashastr police bal (siepief) carmikon samet vibhinn karmchaariyon par asar daalane vaale kuch anya nirnay bhi liye gaye hai, jinamein nimnlikhit shaamil hai
 • Gratuity limit has been increased from Rs 10 lakh to Rs 20 lakh
 jab bhi die 50 pratishat bad jayega tab gracuty kii seemaa 25 pratishat bad jaaegi
 • a general arrangement has been made for the payment of lump sum compensation for civil and defense personnel, which will be payable to their families and under this, the current rates will be increased from Rs 10-20 lakhs to Rs 25-45 lakhs for different categories
 has given
 • raksha balon ke karmiyon kii vibhinn shreniyon ke liye sainya seva vetan kii daren 1000, 2000, 4200 evam 6000 rupee se sanshodhit karke kramash: 3600, 5200, 10800 evam 15500 rupee kar di gai hai
 8
 cabinet ne awaas nirmaan se judi agrim raashi ko 7
 The Commission's recommendation to increase from Rs 50 lakh to Rs 25 lakh has also been approved
 karmchaariyon ko koi dikkat na ho, yah sunishchit karne ke liye 4 byaaj mukt agrimon ko barkaraar rakhaa gaya he, jinamein chikitsa ilaaj ke liye agrim, tour / sthanantaran ke liye tie, mritak karmchaariyon ke parivaar ke liye tie or altisi shaamil hai
 All other interest free advances have been discontinued
 9

 isse pehle karnataka main varisht kannada lekhak kalburgi kii hatya ke maamle main aropiyon kii giraftaar main deree se naaraaz kannada bhashaa ke 6 lekhakon ne kannada sahitya academy kaa puraskaar lautaa diya tha
 Veeranna Madivalrati Satish Javre Goudasangamesh Menasikhani Hanumant haligerishree Devi v Alurchidanand mohammad tughlak charitrik virodhabhas main jenevaala ek aisa badshaah tha jise itihaaskaaron ne uski sanakon ke liye khabti qaraar diya
 Which changed the capital due to its whims and made the value of copper coin equal to that of silver coin
 lekin apane chaaron ore kattar mazahabi deevaaron se ghira tughlak kuch or bhi tha
 He had sought a person beyond religion
 hindu or musalmaan donon uski nazar main ek the
 The erstwhile mentality rejected this recognition of Tughlaq and this 'rejection' rode on Tughlaq's head as a ghost of whims
 girish karnad ne apane is charchit naatak 'tughlak' kaa kathanak maatr tughlak ke gun-dosha tak hi simit nahin he
 It also expresses the circumstances and the sentiments of the time, due to which the contemplation of the man of that time was dwarfed and in the confrontation of religion and politics, each one only wants to straighten his owl
 maharashtra main janme girish karnad, ek behad charchit va prabhaavshaalee lekhak, kalakaar va nirdeshak the
 His mother tongue was Kannada
 ganit kii sarvocch pariksha main safal hokar ‘hodes scollar’ ke rup main vah oxford gaye
 In 1963, he resigned after getting a job at Oxford University Press, Madras in 1970 after getting a 'language Fellowship', where his independent writing began
 unka pehla naatak yayati 1968 main chapa or charchaa kaa vishay bana

 vajan badhane ke alaava motaape ke do aam dushprabhav liver main vasa kaa sanchayan or insulin pratirodh kshamta badha dena he
 'researchers fed a high-fat diet to a group of mice for 15 weeks, while they were also given a CGA solution twice every week

 Know here 7 things related to Maulana Abul Kalam Azad's life: 1
 moulana saiyad abul kalam gulam muhiyuddeen ahamed bin khayruddin al-hossain aaazaad ko puri duniya moulana aaazaad ke naam se jaanati he
 He was an Indian Muslim scholar and freedom fighter as well as one of the senior leaders of the Congress during the Indian independence movement
 2
 Maulana Azad was born on 11 November 1888 in Mecca
 unke pita kaa naam mohammad khayruddin tha, jo ek muslim vidwaan the
 3
 vah aazaadee ke baad uttar pradesh ke rampur jile se 1952 main saansad chune gaye or bharat ke pehle shiksha mantri bane
 4
 aaazaad bharat ke shiksha mantri rahete hue moulana aaazaad ne rashtriya shiksha pranali banaai
 Free primary education was his main objective
 5
 The establishment of the Indian Institute of Technology (IIT) and University Grants Commission (UGC) goes to Maulana Azad
 6
 He also established excellent institutions like Sangeet Natak Akademi (1953), Sahitya Akademi (1954) and Lalitkala Academy (1954) for the development of education and culture
 7
 Maulana Azad was posthumously awarded the Bharat Ratna, India's highest civilian honor, in 1922, for his outstanding contribution in the field of education

 relijase pehle film ke gane bhi hit nahin ho paae hai or filmakan ke dauraan vah bhi niraash karte hai

 kendriya bank kii samiksha rapat main kaha gaya he ki farvari 2013 main sakal vastuon ke thok mulya suchakank par aadhaarit mudrasphiti bad kar 6
 84, which turned out to be 6 in January
 6 fisad thi
 Apparently this seems to be the effect of the revision (increase) in administered prices of petroleum products
 saath hi dhaatu, kapadaa or rabar utpaadon kii keemat main kami ke maddenjar sitambar 2012 main shuru hui kendriya mudrasphiti (vinirmit utpaadon kii mudrasphiti) main kami jari rahi or farvari main yah 3
 Remained at 8 percent
 haalanki arabiai ne kaha ki khudara mudrasphiti abhi bhi chintajanak daayre main bani he jo farvari 2013 main 10
 It was at the level of 9 percent
 kendriya bank ne kaha he ki khaadya utpaadon kii oonchi keemat, nunatam samarthan mulya badhaane ke kaaran badha dabaav or thok evam khudara mudrasphiti ke bich kii hode se bhi mudrasphiti pratyaasha par asar pad rahaa he
 The RBI has suggested the government to be cautious in raising the minimum support price for agricultural products as it has an impact on gross inflation
 arabiai ne madhya timahi samiksha ke drushtikon main kaha ki vaishvik str par jinson kii keemat main kami or gharelu bazaar main maang kam hone ke kaaran companiyon kii keemat badhaane kii kshamta kam hone ke kaaran vinirmit utpaadon kii mudrasphiti kam ho rahi he
 The comments haalanki khaadya mudrasphiti main lagaataar badhotaree ke kaaran thok mulya aadhaarit sakal mudrasphiti daayre se upar he or upabhokta mulya mudrasphiti dahaai ank main he
 The central bank said that managing inflation overall has become a complex process and there is a need to address supply side problems
 bhartiya rigerv bank (arabiai) ne maudrik niti kii mangalvaar ko jari madhya timahi samiksha main kaha ki kshetravaar str par maang or aapurti ke asantulan, vastuon ke prashasit mulyon main vruddhi or iske parinami prabhaavon ke maddenjar sakal mudrasphiti thodaa ghat bad ke saath maujuuda str par bani rah sakati he
 The central bank's review report said that in February 2013, inflation based on the wholesale price index of gross goods increased to 6
 84 par ho gai jo janvari main 6
 It was 6 percent
 prakatat: yah petroleum utpaadon ke prashasit mulyon main sanshodhan (vruddhi) kaa prabhaav lagata he
 At the same time, the central inflation (inflation of manufactured products) started in September 2012 in view of the decrease in the price of metals, textiles and rubber products continued and in February it was 3
 8 fisad par rahi
 However, the RBI said that retail inflation still remained in a worrying range, 10 in February 2013
 9 fisad ke str par rahi
 The central bank has said that inflationary expectations are also being impacted by the high price of food products, increased pressure on raising the minimum support price and the competition between wholesale and retail inflation
 arabiai ne sarkaar se krishi utpaadon ke nunatam samarthan mulya ko badhaane ke maamle main saavdhaanee baratane kaa suzav diya he kyonki iskaa sakal mudrasphiti par asar hota he
 In its mid-quarter review outlook, the RBI said that the inflation in manufactured products is coming down due to the reduction in the price of commodities globally and the ability of companies to increase prices due to reduced demand in the domestic market
 tippaniyan However, due to continuous increase in food inflation, wholesale price based gross inflation is above the ceiling and consumer price inflation is in double digits
 kendriya bank ne kaha ki kul milakar mudrasphiti kaa prabandhan jatil prakriya ban gaya he or aapurti paksh kii dikkaton ko dur karne kii aavashyaktaa jaahir hoti he

 In today's special program, Sidhi Baat, Delhi Chief Minister Sheila Dikshit gave her impeccable opinion about India Today Group editorial director Prabhu Chawla from Jagdish Tytler case to politics and Congress party
 gauratlab he ki shila dikshit lagaataar teesri baar dilli kii mukhyamantri bani hai or loksabhaa chunaavon ke maddenjar dilli ke baahar bhi congress ke liye prachaar kar rahi hai
 On this, Sheela says that she has a relationship with Uttar Pradesh, she is the daughter-in-law of Uttar Pradesh, so she is going there for campaigning
 jagadish titalar se tikat waapas liye jane ke maamle main shila ne kaha ki titalar ko sarvasammati se tikat diya gaya tha or sarvasammati se hi tikat waapas bhi le liya gaya
 He said that the Tytler case was made a deliberate issue
 shila ne kaha ki akali dal or bhaajapa ko pataa tha ki congress punjab main acha karne vaali he isliye unhone titalar ke maamle ko mudda banaaya
 He justified the Congress decision to withdraw the ticket from Tytler and said that electoral interests are also important for every party
 unhone kaha ki is maamle main party ne darkar koi faisla nahin liya balki janata kii aawaaj suni
 When asked if Tytler had to be removed due to the shoe case, he said that the same episode provoked public anger
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki janata dwaara virodh karne kaa yah tarika galat he
 When asked if the way shoes and slippers are being thrown at the leaders, it does not seem that the distance between the leader and the public is increasing, Sheila said that it is not so
 is baar loksabhaa chunaav main kai amir ummidavaar bhi chunaav maidan main hai
 Congress also has many millionaire candidates
 is par shila dikshit kaa kahana he ki congress amiron kii party nahin he lekin haa kuch paise waalon ko raajnneeti kaa chaska jarur laga he
 On the increasing number of criminal types of people in politics, Sheila said that this is harming Indian politics and they are totally against it
 unhone yahaan tak kaha ki jin ummidavaaron kii chhavi kharaab ho unako bhi tikat dene se bachanaa chahie
 When asked whether the Congress was expected to become Prime Minister in future, except for a member of the Gandhi family and not, Sheila said that no one knew that Manmohan Singh would become Prime Minister
 lekin sonia gandhi ne manmohan singh ko pradhanmantri banaaya
 Therefore, what will happen in future cannot be said and anyone can become PM on behalf of the party
